\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
API headers for the mmg3d library. 

\begin{DoxyAuthor}{Author}
Algiane Froehly (Inria/\+UBordeaux) 
\end{DoxyAuthor}
\begin{DoxyVersion}{Version}
5 
\end{DoxyVersion}
\begin{DoxyDate}{Date}
01 2014 
\end{DoxyDate}
\begin{DoxyCopyright}{Copyright}
GNU Lesser General Public License. 
\end{DoxyCopyright}
\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
To keep the genheader working, don\textquotesingle{}t break line between the enum name and the opening brace (it creates errors under windows) 

Use the MMG3\+D\+\_\+ prefix\+: MMG5\+\_\+ prefix will became obsolete...
\end{DoxyWarning}

\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{comment}{/* Name and path of the mesh file */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \mbox{\hyperlink{API__functionsf__3d_8c_a539b7c333f2633a43adfe1fcb5b0430b}{filename}} = (\textcolor{keywordtype}{char} *) calloc(strlen(argv[1]) + 1, \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(char));}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ( \mbox{\hyperlink{API__functionsf__3d_8c_a539b7c333f2633a43adfe1fcb5b0430b}{filename}} == NULL ) \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{  \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{  fileout = (\textcolor{keywordtype}{char} *) calloc(strlen(argv[2]) + 1, \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(char));}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ( fileout == NULL ) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{    perror(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}  \#\# Memory problem: calloc"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{    exit(EXIT\_FAILURE);}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{  strcpy(fileout,argv[2]);}

\DoxyCodeLine{  mmgSol  = NULL;}

\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} ( ier /= 1 ) \textcolor{keyword}{CALL }exit(104)}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keyword}{CALL }mmg3d\_set\_triangle(mmgmesh,  5\_immg,  1\_immg, 8\_immg, ref, 7\_immg,ier)}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} ( ier /= 1 ) \textcolor{keyword}{CALL }exit(104)}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keyword}{CALL }mmg3d\_set\_triangle(mmgmesh,  7\_immg,  6\_immg, 8\_immg, ref, 8\_immg,ier)}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} ( ier /= 1 ) \textcolor{keyword}{CALL }exit(104)}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keyword}{CALL }mmg3d\_set\_triangle(mmgmesh,  4\_immg,  3\_immg, 8\_immg, ref, 9\_immg,ier)}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} ( ier /= 1 ) \textcolor{keyword}{CALL }exit(104)}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keyword}{CALL }mmg3d\_set\_triangle(mmgmesh,  2\_immg,  3\_immg, 4\_immg, ref,10\_immg,ier)}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} ( ier /= 1 ) \textcolor{keyword}{CALL }exit(104)}
\DoxyCodeLine{  ref = 4}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keyword}{CALL }mmg3d\_set\_triangle(mmgmesh,  9\_immg,  3\_immg, 2\_immg, ref,11\_immg,ier)}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} ( ier /= 1 ) \textcolor{keyword}{CALL }exit(104)}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keyword}{CALL }mmg3d\_set\_triangle(mmgmesh, 11\_immg,  9\_immg,12\_immg, ref,12\_immg,ier)}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} ( ier /= 1 ) \textcolor{keyword}{CALL }exit(104)}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keyword}{CALL }mmg3d\_set\_triangle(mmgmesh,  7\_immg, 11\_immg,12\_immg, ref,13\_immg,ier)}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} ( ier /= 1 ) \textcolor{keyword}{CALL }exit(104)}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keyword}{CALL }mmg3d\_set\_triangle(mmgmesh,  6\_immg,  7\_immg,10\_immg, ref,14\_immg,ier)}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} ( ier /= 1 ) \textcolor{keyword}{CALL }exit(104)}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keyword}{CALL }mmg3d\_set\_triangle(mmgmesh,  6\_immg, 10\_immg, 9\_immg, ref,15\_immg,ier)}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} ( ier /= 1 ) \textcolor{keyword}{CALL }exit(104)}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keyword}{CALL }mmg3d\_set\_triangle(mmgmesh,  6\_immg,  9\_immg, 2\_immg, ref,16\_immg,ier)}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} ( ier /= 1 ) \textcolor{keyword}{CALL }exit(104)}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keyword}{CALL }mmg3d\_set\_triangle(mmgmesh, 12\_immg, 10\_immg, 7\_immg, ref,17\_immg,ier)}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} ( ier /= 1 ) \textcolor{keyword}{CALL }exit(104)}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keyword}{CALL }mmg3d\_set\_triangle(mmgmesh, 12\_immg,  9\_immg,10\_immg, ref,18\_immg,ier)}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} ( ier /= 1 ) \textcolor{keyword}{CALL }exit(104)}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keyword}{CALL }mmg3d\_set\_triangle(mmgmesh,  3\_immg, 11\_immg, 7\_immg, ref,19\_immg,ier)}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} ( ier /= 1 ) \textcolor{keyword}{CALL }exit(104)}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keyword}{CALL }mmg3d\_set\_triangle(mmgmesh,  9\_immg, 11\_immg, 3\_immg, ref,20\_immg,ier)}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} ( ier /= 1 ) \textcolor{keyword}{CALL }exit(104)}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{  np = 12}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keyword}{CALL }mmg3d\_set\_solsize(mmgmesh,mmgsol,mmg5\_vertex,np,mmg5\_scalar,ier)}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} ( ier /= 1 ) \textcolor{keyword}{CALL }exit(105)}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keywordflow}{DO} k=1,12}
\DoxyCodeLine{     \textcolor{keyword}{CALL }mmg3d\_set\_scalarsol(mmgsol,0.5d0,k,ier)}
\DoxyCodeLine{     \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} ( ier /= 1 ) \textcolor{keyword}{CALL }exit(106)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keywordflow}{  ENDDO}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keyword}{CALL }mmg3d\_chk\_meshdata(mmgmesh,mmgsol,ier)}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} ( ier /= 1 ) \textcolor{keyword}{CALL }exit(107)}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keyword}{CALL }mmg3d\_mmg3dlib(mmgmesh,mmgsol,ier)}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} ( ier == mmg5\_strongfailure ) \textcolor{keywordflow}{THEN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{    print*,\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}BAD ENDING OF MMG3DLIB: UNABLE TO SAVE MESH"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{    stop mmg5\_strongfailure}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keywordflow}{ELSE} \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} ( ier == mmg5\_lowfailure ) \textcolor{keywordflow}{THEN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{     print*,\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}BAD ENDING OF MMG3DLIB"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keywordflow}{  ENDIF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keyword}{OPEN}(unit=inm,file=trim(adjustl(fileout))//\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}.mesh"{}},form=\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}formatted"{}},status=\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}replace"{}})}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keyword}{WRITE}(inm,*) \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}MeshVersionFormatted 2"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keyword}{WRITE}(inm,*) \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Dimension 3"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keyword}{CALL }mmg3d\_get\_meshsize(mmgmesh,np,ne,\%val(0\_immg),nt,\%val(0\_immg),na,ier)}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} ( ier /= 1 ) \textcolor{keyword}{CALL }exit(108)}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{comment}{! Table to know if a vertex is corner}}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keyword}{ALLOCATE}(corner(np))}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{comment}{! Table to know if a vertex/tetra/tria/edge is required}}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keyword}{ALLOCATE}(required(max(max(np,ne),max(nt,na))))}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{comment}{! Table to know if a coponant is corner and/or required}}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keyword}{ALLOCATE}(ridge(na))}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{  nreq = 0; nc = 0}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keyword}{WRITE}(inm,*)}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keyword}{WRITE}(inm,*) \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Vertices"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keyword}{WRITE}(inm,*) np}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keywordflow}{DO} k=1, np}
\DoxyCodeLine{     \textcolor{keyword}{CALL }mmg3d\_get\_vertex(mmgmesh,point(1),point(2),point(3),\&}
\DoxyCodeLine{          ref,corner(k),required(k),ier)}
\DoxyCodeLine{     \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} ( ier /= 1 ) \textcolor{keyword}{CALL }exit(109)}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{     \textcolor{keyword}{WRITE}(inm,fmt) point(1),point(2),point(3),ref}
\DoxyCodeLine{     \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} ( corner(k)/=0 )  nc=nc+1}
\DoxyCodeLine{     \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} ( required(k)/=0 )  nreq=nreq+1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keywordflow}{  ENDDO}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keyword}{WRITE}(inm,*)}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keyword}{WRITE}(inm,*) \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Corners"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keyword}{WRITE}(inm,*)  nc}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keywordflow}{DO} k=1, np}
\DoxyCodeLine{    \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} ( corner(k)/=0 )  \textcolor{keyword}{WRITE}(inm,*) k}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keywordflow}{  ENDDO}}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keyword}{WRITE}(inm,*)}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keyword}{WRITE}(inm,*) \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}RequiredVertices"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keyword}{WRITE}(inm,*)  nreq}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keywordflow}{DO} k=1,np}
\DoxyCodeLine{    \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} ( required(k)/=0 ) \textcolor{keyword}{WRITE}(inm,*) k}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keywordflow}{  ENDDO}}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keyword}{WRITE}(inm,*)}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keyword}{DEALLOCATE}(corner)}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{  nreq = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keyword}{WRITE}(inm,*) \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Triangles"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keyword}{WRITE}(inm,*) nt}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keywordflow}{DO} k=1,nt}
\DoxyCodeLine{     \textcolor{keyword}{CALL }mmg3d\_get\_triangle(mmgmesh,tria(1),tria(2),tria(3),ref,required(k),ier)}
\DoxyCodeLine{     \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} ( ier /= 1 ) \textcolor{keyword}{CALL }exit(110)}
\DoxyCodeLine{     \textcolor{keyword}{WRITE}(inm,*) tria(1),tria(2),tria(3),ref}
\DoxyCodeLine{     \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} ( required(k)/=0 )  nreq=nreq+1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keywordflow}{  ENDDO}}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keyword}{WRITE}(inm,*)}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keyword}{WRITE}(inm,*) \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}RequiredTriangles"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keyword}{WRITE}(inm,*) nreq}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keywordflow}{DO} k=1,nt}
\DoxyCodeLine{    \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} ( required(k)/=0 ) \textcolor{keyword}{WRITE}(inm,*) k}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keywordflow}{  ENDDO}}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keyword}{WRITE}(inm,*)}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{  nreq = 0;nr = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keyword}{WRITE}(inm,*) \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Edges"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keyword}{WRITE}(inm,*) na}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keywordflow}{DO} k=1,na}
\DoxyCodeLine{     \textcolor{keyword}{CALL }mmg3d\_get\_edge(mmgmesh,edge(1),edge(2),ref,ridge(k),required(k),ier)}
\DoxyCodeLine{     \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} ( ier /= 1 ) \textcolor{keyword}{CALL }exit(111)}
\DoxyCodeLine{     \textcolor{keyword}{WRITE}(inm,*) edge(1),edge(2),ref}
\DoxyCodeLine{     \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} ( ridge(k)/=0 )     nr = nr+1}
\DoxyCodeLine{     \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} ( required(k)/=0 )  nreq = nreq+1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keywordflow}{  ENDDO}}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keyword}{WRITE}(inm,*)}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keyword}{WRITE}(inm,*) \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}RequiredEdges"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keyword}{WRITE}(inm,*) nreq}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keywordflow}{DO} k=1,na}
\DoxyCodeLine{    \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} ( required(k) /=0 ) \textcolor{keyword}{WRITE}(inm,*) k}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keywordflow}{  ENDDO}}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keyword}{WRITE}(inm,*)}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keyword}{WRITE}(inm,*) \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Ridges"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keyword}{WRITE}(inm,*) nr}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keywordflow}{DO} k=1,na}
\DoxyCodeLine{    \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} ( ridge(k) /=0 ) \textcolor{keyword}{WRITE}(inm,*) k}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keywordflow}{  ENDDO}}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keyword}{WRITE}(inm,*)}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{  nreq = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keyword}{WRITE}(inm,*) \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Tetrahedra"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keyword}{WRITE}(inm,*) ne}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keywordflow}{DO} k=1,ne}
\DoxyCodeLine{     \textcolor{keyword}{CALL }mmg3d\_get\_tetrahedron(mmgmesh,tetra(1),tetra(2),tetra(3),tetra(4),\&}
\DoxyCodeLine{          ref,required(k),ier)}
\DoxyCodeLine{    \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} ( ier /= 1 ) \textcolor{keyword}{CALL }exit(112)}
\DoxyCodeLine{    \textcolor{keyword}{WRITE}(inm,*) tetra(1),tetra(2),tetra(3),tetra(4),ref}
\DoxyCodeLine{    \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} ( required(k) /= 0 )  nreq = nreq+1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keywordflow}{  ENDDO}}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keyword}{WRITE}(inm,*)}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keyword}{WRITE}(inm,*) \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}RequiredTetrahedra"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keyword}{WRITE}(inm,*) nreq}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keywordflow}{DO} k=1,ne}
\DoxyCodeLine{    \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} ( required(k) /= 0 ) \textcolor{keyword}{WRITE}(inm,*) k}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keywordflow}{  ENDDO}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keyword}{WRITE}(inm,*) \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}End"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keyword}{CLOSE}(inm)}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keyword}{DEALLOCATE}(required)}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keyword}{DEALLOCATE}(ridge)}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keyword}{OPEN}(unit=inm,file=trim(adjustl(fileout))//\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}.sol"{}},form=\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}formatted"{}},status=\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}replace"{}})}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keyword}{WRITE}(inm,*) \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}MeshVersionFormatted 2"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keyword}{WRITE}(inm,*) \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Dimension 3"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keyword}{WRITE}(inm,*)}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keyword}{CALL }mmg3d\_get\_solsize(mmgmesh,mmgsol,typentity,np,typsol,ier)}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} ( ier /= 1 ) \textcolor{keyword}{CALL }exit(113)}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} ( ( typentity /= mmg5\_vertex ) .OR. ( typsol /= mmg5\_scalar ) ) \textcolor{keywordflow}{THEN}}
\DoxyCodeLine{     \textcolor{keyword}{CALL }exit(114);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keywordflow}{  ENDIF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keyword}{WRITE}(inm,*) \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}SolAtVertices"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keyword}{WRITE}(inm,*) np}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keyword}{WRITE}(inm,*) \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}1 1"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keyword}{WRITE}(inm,*)}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keywordflow}{DO} k=1,np}
\DoxyCodeLine{     \textcolor{keyword}{CALL }mmg3d\_get\_scalarsol(mmgsol,sol,ier)}
\DoxyCodeLine{     \textcolor{keywordflow}{IF} ( ier /= 1 ) \textcolor{keyword}{CALL }exit(115)}
\DoxyCodeLine{     \textcolor{keyword}{WRITE}(inm,*) sol}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keywordflow}{  ENDDO}}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keyword}{WRITE}(inm,*)}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keyword}{WRITE}(inm,*) \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}End"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keyword}{CLOSE}(inm)}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{keyword}{CALL }mmg3d\_free\_all(mmg5\_arg\_start, \&}
\DoxyCodeLine{       mmg5\_arg\_ppmesh,mmgmesh,mmg5\_arg\_ppmet,mmgsol, \&}
\DoxyCodeLine{       mmg5\_arg\_end)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{END PROGRAM }\mbox{\hyperlink{mmg2d_8c_a0ddf1224851353fc92bfbff6f499fa97}{main}}}

\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{comment}{/* args of InitMesh:}}

\DoxyCodeLine{    exit(EXIT\_FAILURE);}

\DoxyCodeLine{  \textcolor{comment}{/* Be careful if you change the hausdorff number (or gradation value)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{comment}{     between 2 run: the information of the previous hausdorff number}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{comment}{     (resp. gradation) is contained in the metric computed during}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{comment}{     the previous run.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{comment}{     Then, you can not grow up the hausdorff value (resp. gradation) without}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMG3D\_Compute\_eigenv()}{MMG3D\_Compute\_eigenv()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{mmg3d__export_8h_acf696c563c6a676b828e3a11ed9295d5}{LIBMMG3\+D\+\_\+\+EXPORT}} int MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+Compute\+\_\+eigenv (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{double}]{m\mbox{[}6\mbox{]},  }\item[{double}]{lambda\mbox{[}3\mbox{]},  }\item[{double}]{vp\mbox{[}3\mbox{]}\mbox{[}3\mbox{]} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em m} & upper part of a symetric matric diagonalizable in $\vert$R \\
\hline
{\em lambda} & array of the metric eigenvalues \\
\hline
{\em vp} & array of the metric eigenvectors\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
the order of the eigenvalues
\end{DoxyReturn}
Compute the real eigenvalues and eigenvectors of a symetric matrice m whose upper part is provided (m11, m12, m13, m22, m23, m33 in this order). lambda\mbox{[}0\mbox{]} is the eigenvalue associated to the eigenvector ( v\mbox{[}0\mbox{]}\mbox{[}0\mbox{]}, v\mbox{[}0,1\mbox{]}, v\mbox{[}0,2\mbox{]} ) in C and to the eigenvector v(1,\+:) in fortran lambda\mbox{[}1\mbox{]} is the eigenvalue associated to the eigenvector ( v\mbox{[}1\mbox{]}\mbox{[}0\mbox{]}, v\mbox{[}1,1\mbox{]}, v\mbox{[}1,2\mbox{]} ) in C and to the eigenvector v(2,\+:) in fortran lambda\mbox{[}2\mbox{]} is the eigenvalue associated to the eigenvector ( v\mbox{[}2\mbox{]}\mbox{[}0\mbox{]}, v\mbox{[}2,1\mbox{]}, v\mbox{[}2,2\mbox{]} ) in C and to the eigenvector v(3,\+:) in fortran

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
Fortran interface\+: \begin{quote}
 SUBROUTINE MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+COMPUTE\+\_\+\+EIGENV(m,lambda,vp,retval)~\newline

 REAL(KIND=8), INTENT(\+OUT) \+:: lambda($\ast$),vp($\ast$)~\newline
 INTEGER, INTENT(\+OUT) \+:: retval~\newline
 END SUBROUTINE~\newline
\end{quote}

\end{DoxyRemark}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{mmg3d__export_8h_acf696c563c6a676b828e3a11ed9295d5}{LIBMMG3\+D\+\_\+\+EXPORT}} int MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+Get\+\_\+adja\+Tet (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{kel,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{listet\mbox{[}4\mbox{]} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Return adjacent elements of a tetrahedron. 

Utils 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer toward the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em kel} & tetrahedron index. \\
\hline
{\em listet} & pointer toward the table of the 4 tetra adjacent to {\itshape kel}. (the index is 0 if there is no adjacent) \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
1.
\end{DoxyReturn}
Find the indices of the 4 adjacent elements of tetrahedron {\itshape kel}. $listet[i] = 0$ if the $i^{th}$ face has no adjacent element (so we are on a boundary face).

Fortran interface\+: \begin{quote}

 INTEGER, INTENT(\+OUT) \+:: retval~\newline
 END SUBROUTINE~\newline
\end{quote}

\index{libmmg3d.h@{libmmg3d.h}!MMG3D\_Get\_numberOfNonBdyTriangles@{MMG3D\_Get\_numberOfNonBdyTriangles}}
\index{MMG3D\_Get\_numberOfNonBdyTriangles@{MMG3D\_Get\_numberOfNonBdyTriangles}!libmmg3d.h@{libmmg3d.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMG3D\_Get\_numberOfNonBdyTriangles()}{MMG3D\_Get\_numberOfNonBdyTriangles()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{mmg3d__export_8h_acf696c563c6a676b828e3a11ed9295d5}{LIBMMG3\+D\+\_\+\+EXPORT}} int MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+Get\+\_\+number\+Of\+Non\+Bdy\+Triangles (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{nb\+\_\+tria }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer toward the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em nb\+\_\+tria} & pointer toward the number of non boundary triangles. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if failed, 1 otherwise.
\end{DoxyReturn}
Get the number of non boundary triangles (for DG methods for example). A triangle is boundary if it is located at the interface of 2 domains with different references or if it belongs to one tetra only. Append these triangles to the list of triangles.

\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
reallocate the triangle array and append the internal triangles. This may modify the behaviour of other functions.
\end{DoxyWarning}
\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
Fortran interface\+: \begin{quote}
 SUBROUTINE MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+GET\+\_\+\+NUMBEROFNONBDYTRIANGLESS(mesh,nb\+\_\+tria,retval)~\newline

 INTEGER(\+MMG5\+F\+\_\+\+INT), INTENT(\+OUT) \+:: nb\+\_\+tria~\newline
 INTEGER, INTENT(\+OUT) \+:: retval~\newline
 END SUBROUTINE~\newline
\end{quote}

\end{DoxyRemark}
First step\+: Mesh analysis to detect the tetra/prisms boundary faces and to store the info in the xtetra/xprisms structures

Second step\+: Count the number of non boundary faces

Third step\+: Append the non boundary edges to the boundary edges array

Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{libmmg3d__tools_8c_source_l00722}{722}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{libmmg3d__tools_8c_source}{libmmg3d\+\_\+tools.\+c}}.

\hline

\hline

\hline

\hline

\hline

\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMG3D\_Get\_tetrahedra()}{MMG3D\_Get\_tetrahedra()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{mmg3d__export_8h_acf696c563c6a676b828e3a11ed9295d5}{LIBMMG3\+D\+\_\+\+EXPORT}} int MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+Get\+\_\+tetrahedra (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{tetra,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{refs,  }\item[{int $\ast$}]{are\+Required }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer toward the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em tetra} & pointer toward the table of the tetrahedra vertices. Vertices of the $i^{th}$ tetra are stored in tetra\mbox{[}(i-\/1)$\ast$4\mbox{]}@4. \\
\hline
{\em refs} & pointer toward the table of the tetrahedron references. References of the $i^{th}$ tetra is stored in refs\mbox{[}i-\/1\mbox{]}. \\
\hline
{\em are\+Required} & pointer toward the table of the flags saying if the tetrahedra are required. are\+Required\mbox{[}i-\/1\mbox{]}=1 if the $i^{th}$ tetra is required. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if failed, 1 otherwise.
\end{DoxyReturn}
Get vertices and references of the mesh tetrahedra.

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
Fortran interface\+: (commentated in order to allow to pass \%val(0) instead of the refs, are\+Corners or are\+Required arrays)
\end{DoxyRemark}

! END SUBROUTINE~\newline

\index{MMG3D\_Get\_tetsFromTria@{MMG3D\_Get\_tetsFromTria}!libmmg3d.h@{libmmg3d.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMG3D\_Get\_tetsFromTria()}{MMG3D\_Get\_tetsFromTria()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{mmg3d__export_8h_acf696c563c6a676b828e3a11ed9295d5}{LIBMMG3\+D\+\_\+\+EXPORT}} int MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+Get\+\_\+tets\+From\+Tria (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{ktri,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{ktet\mbox{[}2\mbox{]},  }\item[{int}]{iface\mbox{[}2\mbox{]} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer toward the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em ktri} & index of the boundary triangle. \\
\hline
{\em ktet} & array of size 2 that will contain the indices of the tetra (filled by the function). \\
\hline
{\em iface} & pointer toward an array of size 2 that will contains the indices of the faces of the tetras {\itshape ktet}\mbox{[}i\mbox{]} that corresponds to the boundary tria {\itshape ktri}.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if fail, 1 otherwise
\end{DoxyReturn}
Fill {\itshape ktet} by the indices of the tetra to which belong a boundary triangle and {\itshape iface} by the indices of the faces of the tetras that correspond to the triangle. Fill ktet\mbox{[}1\mbox{]} and iface\mbox{[}1\mbox{]} by 0 if the triangle belongs to 1 tetra only.

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
Fortran interface\+: \begin{quote}
 SUBROUTINE MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+GET\+\_\+\+TETSFROMTRIA(mesh,ktri,ktet,iface,retval)~\newline

 INTEGER(\+MMG5\+F\+\_\+\+INT), INTENT(\+IN) \+:: ktri~\newline
 INTEGER(\+MMG5\+F\+\_\+\+INT), DIMENSION(2), INTENT(\+OUT)\+:: ktet~\newline
 INTEGER, DIMENSION(2), INTENT(\+OUT) \+:: iface~\newline
 INTEGER, INTENT(\+OUT) \+:: retval~\newline
 END SUBROUTINE~\newline
\end{quote}

\end{DoxyRemark}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMG3D\_Init\_mesh()}{MMG3D\_Init\_mesh()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{mmg3d__export_8h_acf696c563c6a676b828e3a11ed9295d5}{LIBMMG3\+D\+\_\+\+EXPORT}} int MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+Init\+\_\+mesh (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const int}]{starter,  }\item[{}]{... }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em starter} & dummy argument used to initialize the variadic argument list \\
\hline
{\em ...} & variadic arguments that depend to the library function that you want to call.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
For the MMG3\+D\+\_\+mmg3dlib function, you need to call the {\itshape MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+Init\+\_\+mesh} function with the following arguments \+: MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+Init\+\_\+mesh(\+MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+start,\+MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+pp\+Mesh, \&your\+\_\+mesh, MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+pp\+Met \+MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+pp\+Met, \&your\+\_\+metric,\+MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+end).

For the MMG3\+D\+\_\+mmg3dls function, you need to call the {\itshape MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+Init\+\_\+mesh} function with the following arguments \+: MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+Init\+\_\+mesh(\+MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+start,\+MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+pp\+Mesh, \&your\+\_\+mesh, MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+pp\+Ls, \&your\+\_\+level\+\_\+set,\+MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+end).

For the MMG3\+D\+\_\+mmg3dmov function, you must call \+: MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+Init\+\_\+mesh(\+MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+start,\+MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+pp\+Mesh, \&your\+\_\+mesh, \+MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+pp\+Met,\&empty\+\_\+metric,\+MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+pp\+Disp, \&your\+\_\+displacement, \+MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+end).

Here,{\itshape your\+\_\+mesh} is a {\itshape MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}, {\itshape your\+\_\+metric} {\itshape your\+\_\+level\+\_\+set} and {\itshape your\+\_\+displacement} are {\itshape MMG5\+\_\+p\+Sol}.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
1 if success, 0 if fail
\end{DoxyReturn}
MMG structures allocation and initialization.

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
No fortran interface to allow variadic arguments.
\end{DoxyRemark}
\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
detected bugs\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item some points along open-\/boundaries end up with a normal (while they should not) 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyWarning}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{mmg3d__export_8h_acf696c563c6a676b828e3a11ed9295d5}{LIBMMG3\+D\+\_\+\+EXPORT}} int MMG3\+D\+\_\+load\+Vtk\+Mesh (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a73ac506fe087cc604bb892e46373719a}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Sol}}}]{sol,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{filename }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer toward the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em sol} & pointer toward the solution structure. \\
\hline
{\em filename} & name of file.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if file is not found, -\/1 if fail for another reason (mem lack, file format...), 1 if success.
\end{DoxyReturn}
Read mesh and 0 or 1 data at VTK file format (.vtu extension). We read only low-\/order points, edges, tria, quadra, tetra and prisms. Point and cell references must be stored in Point\+Data or Cell\+Data whose names contains the \char`\"{}medit\+:ref\char`\"{} keyword.

 INTEGER, INTENT(\+IN) \+:: strlen0~\newline
 INTEGER, INTENT(\+OUT) \+:: retval~\newline
 END SUBROUTINE~\newline
\end{quote}

Checks 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer toward the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em met} & pointer toward the sol structure (metric). \\
\hline
{\em sol} & pointer toward the sol structure (ls or displacement). \\
\hline
{\em critmin} & minimum quality for elements. \\
\hline
{\em lmin} & minimum edge length. \\
\hline
{\em lmax} & maximum ede length. \\
\hline
{\em eltab} & table of invalid elements. \\
\hline
{\em met\+Rid\+Typ} & Type of storage of ridges metrics\+: 0 for classic storage (before the MMG5\+\_\+defsiz call), 1 for special storage (after this call).\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
Search invalid elements (in term of quality or edge length).

\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMG3D\_searchlen()}{MMG3D\_searchlen()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{mmg3d__export_8h_acf696c563c6a676b828e3a11ed9295d5}{LIBMMG3\+D\+\_\+\+EXPORT}} int MMG3\+D\+\_\+searchlen (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a73ac506fe087cc604bb892e46373719a}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Sol}}}]{met,  }\item[{double}]{lmin,  }\item[{double}]{lmax,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{eltab,  }\item[{int8\+\_\+t}]{met\+Rid\+Typ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer toward the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em met} & pointer toward the sol structure. \\
\hline
{\em lmin} & minimum edge length. \\
\hline
{\em lmax} & maximum ede length. \\
\hline
{\em eltab} & table of invalid elements. \\
\hline
{\em met\+Rid\+Typ} & Type of storage of ridges metrics\+: 0 for classic storage (before the MMG5\+\_\+defsiz call), 1 for special storage (after this call).\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
1 if success, 0 otherwise.
\end{DoxyReturn}
Store in {\itshape eltab} elements which have edge lengths shorter than {\itshape lmin} or longer than {\itshape lmax}, {\itshape eltab} is allocated and could contain {\itshape mesh-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}ne} elements.

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
Fortran interface\+: \begin{quote}
 SUBROUTINE MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+SEARCHLEN(mesh,met,lmin,lmax,eltab,metridtyp,retval)~\newline

 REAL(KIND=8), INTENT(\+IN) \+:: lmin,lmax~\newline
 INTEGER(\+MMG5\+F\+\_\+\+INT),DIMENSION($\ast$), INTENT(\+OUT) \+:: eltab~\newline
 INTEGER, INTENT(\+IN) \+:: metridtyp~\newline
 INTEGER, INTENT(\+OUT) \+:: retval~\newline
 END SUBROUTINE~\newline
\end{quote}

\end{DoxyRemark}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMG3D\_searchqua()}{MMG3D\_searchqua()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{mmg3d__export_8h_acf696c563c6a676b828e3a11ed9295d5}{LIBMMG3\+D\+\_\+\+EXPORT}} void MMG3\+D\+\_\+searchqua (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a73ac506fe087cc604bb892e46373719a}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Sol}}}]{met,  }\item[{double}]{critmin,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{eltab,  }\item[{int8\+\_\+t}]{met\+Rid\+Typ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer toward the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em met} & pointer toward the sol structure. \\
\hline
{\em critmin} & minimum quality for elements. \\
\hline
{\em eltab} & pointer toward the table of invalid elements. \\
\hline
{\em met\+Rid\+Typ} & Type of storage of ridges metrics\+: 0 for classic storage (before the MMG5\+\_\+defsiz call), 1 for special storage (after this call).\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
Store elements which have worse quality than {\itshape critmin} in {\itshape eltab}, {\itshape eltab} is allocated and could contain {\itshape mesh-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}ne} elements.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMG3D\_Set\_lsBaseReference()}{MMG3D\_Set\_lsBaseReference()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{mmg3d__export_8h_acf696c563c6a676b828e3a11ed9295d5}{LIBMMG3\+D\+\_\+\+EXPORT}} int MMG3\+D\+\_\+\+Set\+\_\+ls\+Base\+Reference (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a73ac506fe087cc604bb892e46373719a}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Sol}}}]{sol,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{br }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer toward the mesh structure. \\
\hline
{\em sol} & pointer toward the sol structure. \\
\hline
{\em br} & new level-\/set base reference. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if failed, 1 otherwise.
\end{DoxyReturn}
Set a new level-\/set base reference of ref {\itshape br} in ls discretization mode. Base references are boundary conditions to which implicit domain can be attached. All implicit volumes that are not attached to listed base references are deleted as spurious volumes by the {\itshape rmc} option.

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
Fortran interface\+: \begin{quote}

 INTEGER(\+MMG5\+F\+\_\+\+INT) \+:: br~\newline
 INTEGER, INTENT(\+OUT) \+:: retval~\newline
 END SUBROUTINE~\newline
\end{quote}

\end{DoxyRemark}
